position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">WebAssembly (Wasm) and asm.js are both technologies designed to run high-performance, low-level code in the browser at near-native speeds</div>. While asm.js was a pioneering "hack" to bridge the gap between JavaScript and native performance, WebAssembly is its standardized, more efficient successor.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Text-based</span>&nbsp;(a strict subset of JavaScript).</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Binary format</span>&nbsp;(compact and efficient).</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Parsing Speed</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); must be parsed like regular JavaScript.</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Fast</span>; designed for rapid decoding and parallel parsing.</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Standardization</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Informal spec primarily driven by Mozilla.</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">W3C Standard</span>&nbsp;supported by all major browsers.</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">File Size</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Larger (requires gzip/minification to be compact).</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Smaller</span>&nbsp;(typically 10-20% smaller than gzipped JS).</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Capabilities</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Limited by JavaScript's syntax and semantics.</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Can introduce features JS cannot, like 64-bit integers.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div></div><hr style="height: 1px; border-right: 0px; border-bottom: 0px; border-left: 0px; border-image: initial; border-top: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); margin-block: 32px;"><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Key Differences</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Execution Model</span>:&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="http://asmjs.org/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">asm.js</a></span>&nbsp;is valid JavaScript code that an engine can optimize if it recognizes the specific patterns. WebAssembly is a completely separate binary instruction format that runs on its own stack-based virtual machine.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Performance Predictability</span>: While asm.js could achieve native speeds, its performance was inconsistent because browsers optimized it differently. WebAssembly provides more&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">predictable performance</span>&nbsp;because it was designed from the ground up as a compilation target.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Startup Time</span>: WebAssembly's binary format allows for&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">streaming compilation</span>, meaning it can be compiled as it downloads. In contrast, asm.js requires the entire text file to be received and parsed before it can be fully optimized.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Tooling</span>: Both are typically used as targets for&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://emscripten.org/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">Emscripten</a></span>, which compiles C/C++ code. Initially, Wasm was "co-expressive" with asm.js, but it has since diverged to support more advanced features like&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">multi-threading</span>.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 109.922px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Stack Overflow</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+7</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">When to Use Which?</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Today,&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly is the industry standard</span>&nbsp;and should be used for all new high-performance web projects.&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">asm.js</span>&nbsp;is largely considered a legacy technology, primarily useful as a fallback for very old browsers that do not support Wasm.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 100.469px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex: 0 0 var(--thumbnail-width); width: var(--thumbnail-width); height: 82px; overflow: hidden; position: relative; --thumbnail-width: 141px;"><div style="position: absolute; display: flex; background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6); color: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 12px; line-height: 16px; letter-spacing: 0.1px; bottom: 4px; left: 4px; padding: 2px 6px 2px 4px; border-radius: 20px; align-items: center; gap: 2px;"><div style="height: 12px;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 12 12" width="12px" fill="currentColor"><path d="M3.5 2.7611V9.2386C3.5 9.77772 4.10085 10.0993 4.54942 9.80023L9.40755 6.56148C9.80832 6.2943 9.80832 5.70539 9.40755 5.43821L4.54942 2.19946C4.10085 1.90041 3.5 2.22198 3.5 2.7611Z"></path></svg></div>19:18</div></div></div></div></li></ul><div style="position: relative; padding: 4px 20px 16px;"><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: stretch; border-radius: 9999px; color: var(--jINu6c); cursor: pointer; display: flex; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; position: relative; background-color: var(--aYn2S); outline: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; min-height: var(--aim-container-min-height); color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">the history</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">The history of high-performance web code is a story of "useful hacks" evolving into a global standard. It began with the need to run complex, desktop-class software (like 3D games) in the browser without slow plugins like Flash or Java</div>.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 111.961px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">WordPress.com</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Timeline of Development</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">2010 – The Origin of Emscripten</span>: Alon Zakai created&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Emscripten</span>, a tool to compile C/C++ into JavaScript. While groundbreaking, the resulting JavaScript was often slow because engines weren't designed for that specific type of code.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">2013 – The "Super Hacky" asm.js</span>: Mozilla engineers released&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">asm.js</span>. It wasn't a new language, but a strict subset of JavaScript that served as a "virtual machine." If a browser recognized the "use asm" pragma, it could skip expensive checks and run the code at near-native speeds.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">2015 – WebAssembly Announced</span>: Despite the success of asm.js, its text-based format was slow to parse, especially on mobile. A cross-browser coalition (Mozilla, Google, Microsoft, and Apple) announced&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly (Wasm)</span>&nbsp;as a new binary successor that combined the best of asm.js and Google's Native Client (PNaCl).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">2017 – The MVP Launch</span>: All four major browsers shipped support for the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly MVP (1.0)</span>. This allowed developers to ship complex apps like Google Earth and Unity-based games to the web with universal support.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">2019 – The Fourth Language</span>: The W3C officially named WebAssembly the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">"fourth language of the web"</span>&nbsp;alongside HTML, CSS, and JavaScript.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">2022–2025 – Modern Standards</span>:</span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Wasm 2.0 (2022–2024)</span>: Added features like&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/WebAssembly" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">SIMD</a></span>&nbsp;for parallel processing and multi-value returns.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Wasm 3.0 (2025)</span>: Introduced 64-bit addressing, native&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Garbage Collection (WasmGC)</span>, and exception handling, allowing high-level languages like Java and Kotlin to run even more efficiently.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 104.086px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Brendan Eich</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+12</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Evolution Summary</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 flex;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; flex-shrink: 1; max-inline-size: 200px;">WordPress.com</span></span></div><div style="margin-inline-start: 8px;"><div tabindex="0" role="button" style="margin: var(--z9dUe--aOgmJd,0); position: relative; display: flex; justify-content: center; align-items: center; cursor: pointer; z-index: 1; outline: 0px;"><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M480-160q-33 0-56.5-23.5T400-240q0-33 23.5-56.5T480-320q33 0 56.5 23.5T560-240q0 33-23.5 56.5T480-160Zm0-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T400-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T480-560q33 0 56.5 23.5T560-480q0 33-23.5 56.5T480-400Zm0-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T400-720q0-33 23.5-56.5T480-800q33 0 56.5 23.5T560-720q0 33-23.5 56.5T480-640Z"></path></svg></div></div></div></div></div></div></li></ul><div style="position: relative; padding: 4px 20px 16px;"><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: stretch; border-radius: 9999px; color: var(--jINu6c); cursor: pointer; display: flex; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; position: relative; background-color: var(--aYn2S); outline: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></body></html>

---

<html><head></head><body><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: auto ease 0s 1 normal none running none; padding-top: 30px; position: relative; opacity: 1; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">how to use asm.js</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">To use&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">asm.js</span>, you typically don't write it by hand. Instead, it is&nbsp;<mark style="border-radius: 4px; background-image: ; background-position-x: ; background-position-y: ; background-size: ; background-repeat: ; background-attachment: ; background-origin: ; background-clip: ; padding: 0px 2px;">used as a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">compile target</span>&nbsp;for low-level languages like C or C++ to run at near-native speeds in the browser</mark>.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 77.3906px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">SitePoint</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">While&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly (Wasm)</span>&nbsp;has largely superseded it for modern performance-critical web tasks, you can still generate and use asm.js using the following methods:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 76.1016px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">YouTube</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. Compile C/C++ to asm.js (Recommended)<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The standard way to use asm.js is through the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Emscripten</span>&nbsp;compiler toolchain.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 75.4531px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">SitePoint</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Install Emscripten:</span>&nbsp;Follow the official&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Emscripten installation guide</span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Compile your code:</span>&nbsp;Run the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">emcc</code>&nbsp;command with the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">-s ASM_JS=1</code>&nbsp;flag to force asm.js output:</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">bash</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code>emcc -O2 -s ASM_JS=1 my_code.cpp -o output.js
</code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Integration:</span>&nbsp;Include the resulting&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">.js</code>&nbsp;file in your HTML. It will automatically initialize the environment and run your compiled functions.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 65.0078px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Reddit</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Manually Writing an asm.js Module<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">If you are experimenting with hand-written asm.js, you must follow a very strict, statically-typed subset of JavaScript.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 108.078px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Stack Overflow</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Define the Module:</span>&nbsp;Wrap your code in a "factory" function that takes up to three arguments:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">stdlib</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">foreign</code>, and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">heap</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Use the Pragma:</span>&nbsp;Start the function with the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">"use asm";</code>&nbsp;string.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Use Type Coercions:</span>&nbsp;You must explicitly "cast" every variable and return value using bitwise operations:</span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Integers:</span>&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">x | 0</code>&nbsp;(bitwise OR with zero).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Doubles:</span>&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">+x</code>&nbsp;(unary plus).</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 81.6875px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Wikipedia</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+7</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Example Template:</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">function</span><span> MyAsmModule(stdlib, foreign, heap) {
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"use asm"</span><span>;
  
  </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Example function: adds two integers</span><span>
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">function</span><span> add(a, b) {
    a = a | </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">0</span><span>;      </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Coerce a to integer</span><span>
    b = b | </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">0</span><span>;      </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Coerce b to integer</span><span>
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> (a + b) | </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">0</span><span>; </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Return result as integer</span><span>
  }
  
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> { add: add };
}

</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Initialization</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">var</span><span> buffer = </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">new</span><span> ArrayBuffer(</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">0x10000</span><span>); </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// The heap memory</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">var</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">module</span><span> = MyAsmModule(window, {}, buffer);
console.log(</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">module</span><span>.add(</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">5</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">10</span><span>)); </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Outputs: 15</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Key Limitations<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">No Garbage Collection:</span>&nbsp;You must manage memory yourself using line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">how fast is it</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">In modern browsers,&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">asm.js</span>&nbsp;typically runs at&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">1.5x to 2x slower than native C++ code</span>. While it is significantly faster than standard, unoptimized JavaScript, it is now generally surpassed by its successor,&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly (Wasm)</span>.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 101.938px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Mozilla Hacks</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Performance Comparisons<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Performance varies based on the browser and the type of task, but common benchmarks show:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Vs. Native C++:</span>&nbsp;Asm.js usually stays within a factor of 2 of native speed. In some highly specific, math-heavy cases (like the Box2D physics engine), it has even approached near-parity with native code.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Vs. Standard JavaScript:</span>&nbsp;Asm.js is much faster, often outperforming idiomatic JS by&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">10x to 40x</span>&nbsp;for heavy computational tasks like image processing or physics simulations.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Vs. WebAssembly:</span>&nbsp;WebAssembly is consistently faster than asm.js, typically by&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">10% to 50%</span>. This is because Wasm uses a binary format that is faster to parse and can access CPU features (like 64-bit integers and SIMD) that asm.js cannot.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 99.5312px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Hacker News</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Why It Is Fast<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Asm.js achieves this speed by using a "statically typed" subset of JavaScript that browsers can optimize ahead of time (AOT):<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 102.477px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Mozilla Hacks</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">No Garbage Collection:</span>&nbsp;It uses a single, fixed-size&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">ArrayBuffer</code>&nbsp;as "manual memory," avoiding the unpredictable pauses of the JavaScript garbage collector.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Predictable Types:</span>&nbsp;Because every variable is explicitly "coerced" (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">x | 0</code>&nbsp;for integers), the engine doesn't have to guess types at runtime.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 98.875px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Hacker News</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Critical Bottleneck: Startup Time<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">While execution is fast,&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">startup time</span>&nbsp;can be a major issue for large asm.js projects. Because it is delivered as plain text, the browser must parse and validate millions of lines of code before it can even begin executing. This is one of the primary reasons the industry shifted to the binary format of&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://webassembly.org/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">WebAssembly</a></span>.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Are you comparing asm.js to WebAssembly for a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">new project</span>, or are you working with a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">legacy codebase</span>?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div><div style="clear: both; display: flex; flex-flow: wrap; row-gap: 16px; margin-block: 18px 0px; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="display: contents;"></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; flex-shrink: 1; width: 652px; align-items: center;"><div style="display: flex;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"><div><svg fill="currentColor" width="20px" height="20px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 -1 13 18"><path d="M1.77734 2.96289C2.10462 2.96289 2.37012 3.22838 2.37012 3.55566C2.37003 3.86235 2.13657 4.11509 1.83789 4.14551L1.7168 4.15137C1.41824 4.18181 1.18479 4.43369 1.18457 display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">If you were to hand-write&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">asm.js</span>, its speed would be significantly faster than standard JavaScript but slightly slower and less predictable than WebAssembly.</div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Performance Breakdown</div><div></div><div style="overflow-x: auto; margin-block: 16px 24px; box-sizing: border-box; scrollbar-width: none; inline-size: calc(100% + 20px); padding-inline-end: 24px;"><table style="border: none; border-collapse: collapse; table-layout: auto; width: 648px;"><tbody><tr><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 16px 8px 0px; text-align: left;">Format</th><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 16px 8px 0px; text-align: left;">Typical Speed (Relative to Native)</th><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 0px; text-align: left;">Key Performance Characteristics</th></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Native (C/C++)</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">1.0x</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Full access to CPU instructions (SIMD, 64-bit ints) and direct memory.</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">1.1x – 1.5x</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Binary format allows for near-instant parsing and better optimization.</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">asm.js</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">1.5x – 2.0x</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Fast execution but hampered by slow text parsing and missing CPU features.</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Normal JS</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">2x – 10x+</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">High variability due to garbage collection and dynamic type checking.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Handwritten asm.js vs. The Rest</div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Vs. Normal JS:</span>&nbsp;Handwritten asm.js is substantially faster for math-heavy tasks because it uses&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">static types</span>&nbsp;(e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">x | 0</code>&nbsp;for integers). This allows the browser to bypass "expensive" steps like type guessing and garbage collection. For small, non-computational tasks, normal JS may actually be faster due to the overhead of setting up the asm.js heap.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Vs. WebAssembly (Wasm):</span>&nbsp;Even the most perfectly handwritten asm.js will usually be&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">30–50% slower</span>&nbsp;than Wasm. Wasm supports features asm.js cannot, such as 64-bit integers and SIMD (Single Instruction, Multiple Data), which can make encryption or image processing up to 4x faster.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Vs. Native:</span>&nbsp;asm.js is remarkably close to native speed for a browser technology, often within a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">2x factor</span>. In rare, extremely optimized cases like the Box2D physics engine, it has reached performance nearly equal to native code.</span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">The "Handwriting" Penalty</div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Writing asm.js by hand is extremely difficult and error-prone. If you miss even one type coercion (like a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">+</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">| 0</code>), the browser will fail to validate the module. If validation fails, the engine falls back to standard JS, and you lose all your performance gains instantly.</div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Would you like to see a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">code comparison</span>&nbsp;of how a simple math function looks in normal JS versus handwritten asm.js?</div><div></div><div><div style="clear: both; display: flex; flex-flow: wrap; row-gap: 16px; margin-block: 18px 0px; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="display: contents;"></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; flex-shrink: 1; width: 652px; align-items: center;"><div style="display: flex;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"><div><svg fill="currentColor" width="20px" animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">give me an example of hand written asm js code which is perf critical</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">A classic example for&nbsp;</div><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">asm.js</code>&nbsp;is a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">vector magnitude calculation</span>&nbsp;(finding the length of a 3D vector). This is "perf-critical" because it’s called millions of times per second in physics engines or 3D games.</div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Here is how you would hand-write it. Notice the "ugly" syntax—every variable must be coerced to a type immediately.</div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">function</span><span> VectorUtils(stdlib, foreign, heap) {
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"use asm"</span><span>;

  </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Link to Math.sqrt from the standard library</span><span>
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">var</span><span> sqrt = stdlib.Math.sqrt;

  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">function</span><span> getMagnitude(x, y, z) {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 1. Coerce inputs to doubles (using unary +)</span><span>
    x = +x;
    y = +y;
    z = +z;

    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 2. Define internal variables with types</span><span>
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">var</span><span> dotProduct = </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">0.0</span><span>;
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">var</span><span> result = </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">0.0</span><span>;

    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 3. Perform math (all operations stay in double-precision)</span><span>
    dotProduct = +(x * x + y * y + z * z);
    
    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 4. Call the linked sqrt function</span><span>
    result = +sqrt(dotProduct);

    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 5. Return as a double</span><span>
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> +result;
  }

  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> { getMagnitude: getMagnitude };
}

</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// --- Initialization ---</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// We pass 'window' as the stdlib to give access to Math functions</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">var</span><span> utils = VectorUtils(window, {}, </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">new</span><span> ArrayBuffer(</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">0x10000</span><span>));

</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Usage</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">var</span><span> len = utils.getMagnitude(</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">3.0</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">4.0</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">0.0</span><span>); 
console.log(len); </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 5</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Why this is "Fast":</div><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">AOT Compilation:</span>&nbsp;When the browser sees&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">"use asm";</code>, it doesn't wait to run the code. it compiles it into machine code&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">immediately</em>&nbsp;because the types are guaranteed.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">No Type Checks:</span>&nbsp;In "Normal JS," the engine asks:&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">"Is&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">x</code>&nbsp;a string? Is it an object?"</em>&nbsp;before adding. In the code above,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">x = +x</code>&nbsp;tells the engine:&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">"This is a float. Period."</em></span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The "Plus" Trick:</span>&nbsp;The&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">+</code>&nbsp;before&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">sqrt</code>&nbsp;and the variables ensures the CPU uses&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">FPU (Floating Point Unit)</span>&nbsp;registers directly, just like C++.</span></li></ol><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">The Catch:</div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">If you forgot a single&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">+</code>&nbsp;or used&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">x = x | 0</code>&nbsp;(integer) by mistake, the browser would throw a console warning:&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">"Asm.js type error: line X: expected double"</span>. It would then treat the whole thing as slow, regular JavaScript.</div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Do you want to see how this same logic would be written in&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly (Wasm)</span>&nbsp;to see the difference in syntax and structure?</div><div></div><div><div style="clear: both; display: flex; flex-flow: wrap; row-gap: 16px; margin-block: 18px 0px; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="display: contents;"></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; flex-shrink: 1; width: 652px; align-items: center;"><div style="display: flex;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"><div><svg fill="currentColor" width="20px" height="20px"
